           </i>

         <script type="text/javascript">
          function validateFormOnSubmit(donateWidget) {
 		var widgetState = donateWidget.donationType.value,
 			origin = widgetState,
 			value = 0,
 			tmpvalue = 0;
 
 		for (var i = 0; i < donateWidget['rnw-amount'].length; i++){
 			if(donateWidget['rnw-amount'][i].checked) {
 				tmpvalue = donateWidget['rnw-amount'][i].value;
 				break;
 			}
 		}
 
         if (tmpvalue == 'custom') {
 		    value = donateWidget.amountCustom.value;
 		} else {
 			value = tmpvalue;
 		}
 
 		//console.log(origin);
 		//console.log(value);
 
 		if (value > 0) {
 			return true;
 		}
 
 		return false;
 	}
         </script>
